<div class=3D"entry-meta"> <span class=3D"posted-on"><time class=3D"entry-date published" datetime= =3D"2022-03-31T20:01:03+08:00" itemprop=3D"datePublished">Publicado em: qui= nta-feira, 31 de mar=C3=A7o de 2022</time></span> <span class=3D"byline"><= span class=3D"author vcard" itemtype=3D"http://schema.org/Person" itemscope= =3D"itemscope" itemprop=3D"author">by <span class=3D"fn n author-name" item= prop=3D"name">Joshua James</span></span></span> </div> </header> =09 <div class=3D"entry-content" itemprop=3D"text"> =09 <p>Como a maioria sabe, o Python 3.7 =C3=A9 a vers=C3=A3o mais antiga do Py= thon atualmente com suporte de seguran=C3=A7a, com muitas portagens ou atua= liza=C3=A7=C3=B5es para 3.8, 3.9 e, mais recentemente, 3.10 com 3.11 no sta= tus RC. Para alguns aplicativos ou frameworks no Ubuntu, pode ser necess=C3= =A1rio instalar o Python 3.7 em seu sistema. Atualmente, o Python 3.7 est= =C3=A1 sendo trabalhado para lan=C3=A7amentos de seguran=C3=A7a at=C3=A9 o = final da vida =C3=BAtil no 6=C2=BA m=C3=AAs de 2023. No entanto, =C3=A9 aco= nselh=C3=A1vel atualizar para vers=C3=B5es mais recentes se voc=C3=AA desen= volver aplicativos o mais r=C3=A1pido poss=C3=ADvel.</p> <p class=3D"gt-block"><em>No tutorial a seguir, voc=C3=AA aprender=C3=A1 co= mo baixar o Python 3.7 mais recente e instalar o formato de arquivo ou usar= um PPA com esta vers=C3=A3o do Python no Ubuntu 20.04 LTS Focal Fossa usan= do o terminal de comando.</em></p> <div id=3D"ez-toc-container" class=3D"ez-toc-v2_0_29 counter-hierarchy coun= ter-numeric ez-toc-transparent"> <p class=3D"ez-toc-title">=C3=8Dndice anal=C3=ADtico</p> <h2><span class=3D"ez-toc-section" id=3D"Update_Ubuntu"></span>Atualize o U= buntu<span class=3D"ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2> <p>Antes de come=C3=A7ar, execute uma atualiza=C3=A7=C3=A3o r=C3=A1pida par= a garantir que seu sistema esteja atualizado para evitar conflitos durante = o tutorial e uma boa manuten=C3=A7=C3=A3o do sistema.</p> <pre class=3D"wp-block-code language-bash" tabindex=3D"0"><code lang=3D"bas= h" class=3D"language-bash"><span class=3D"token function">sudo</span> <span= class=3D"token function">apt</span> update <span class=3D"token operator">= &&</span> <span class=3D"token function">sudo</span> <span class=3D= "token function">apt</span> upgrade</code></pre> <h2><span class=3D"ez-toc-section" id=3D"Install_Python_37_-_PPA_Method"></= span>Instale o Python 3.7 =E2=80=93 M=C3=A9todo PPA<span class=3D"ez-toc-se= ction-end"></span></h2> <div class=3D"code-block code-block-9 code-block-block-9" style=3D"margin: = 0px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; min-height: 310p= x;"> <div><div><iframe data-id=3D"linuxcapable.com_970x90_large_leaderboard_DFP"= frameborder=3D"0" scrolling=3D"no" marginheight=3D"0" marginwidth=3D"0" to= pmargin=3D"0" leftmargin=3D"0" width=3D"1" height=3D"1" data-rendered=3D"tr= ue"></iframe> </div> </div> </div> <p class=3D"gt-block">A primeira e mais f=C3=A1cil solu=C3=A7=C3=A3o para u= su=C3=A1rios do Ubuntu seria importar o <strong><a href=3D"https://launchpa= d.net/~deadsnakes" target=3D"_blank" rel=3D"noreferrer noopener">equipe "mo= rtos"</a></strong> PPA Launchpad. Dado que o 3.7 n=C3=A3o ver=C3=A1 muitas = atualiza=C3=A7=C3=B5es al=C3=A9m de atualiza=C3=A7=C3=B5es de seguran=C3=A7= a urgentes, voc=C3=AA deve instalar o padr=C3=A3o est=C3=A1vel, mas a vers= =C3=A3o noturna ser=C3=A1 discutida para quem preferir; as atualiza=C3=A7= =C3=B5es provavelmente atingir=C3=A3o os dois simultaneamente.</p> <p>Primeiro, instale o pr=C3=A9-requisito para adicionar PPAs personalizado= s.</p> <pre class=3D"wp-block-code language-bash" tabindex=3D"0"><code lang=3D"bas= h" class=3D"language-bash"><span class=3D"token function">sudo</span> <span= class=3D"token function">apt</span> <span class=3D"token function">install= </span> software-properties-common -y</code></pre> <p class=3D"gt-block">Em segundo lugar, adicione o<strong> <mark style=3D"b= ackground-color:var(--contrast-2)" class=3D"has-inline-color has-base-3-col= or">cobras mortas / ppa</mark></strong> =C3=A0 sua lista de fontes do pacot= e APT com o seguinte comando.</p> <pre class=3D"wp-block-code language-bash" tabindex=3D"0"><code lang=3D"bas= h" class=3D"language-bash"><span class=3D"token function">sudo</span> add-a= pt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa -y</code></pre> <div class=3D"code-block code-block-9 code-block-block-9" style=3D"margin: = 0px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; min-height: 310p= x;"> <div><div><iframe data-id=3D"linuxcapable.com_970x90_large_leaderboard_DFP"= frameborder=3D"0" scrolling=3D"no" marginheight=3D"0" marginwidth=3D"0" to= pmargin=3D"0" leftmargin=3D"0" width=3D"1" height=3D"1" data-rendered=3D"tr= ue"></iframe> </div> </div> </div> <p class=3D"gt-block">Depois que o reposit=C3=B3rio for importado, execute = um <strong><mark style=3D"background-color:var(--contrast-2)" class=3D"has-= inline-color has-base-3-color">Atualiza=C3=A7=C3=A3o APT</mark></strong> pa= ra atualizar seu gerenciador de pacotes para refletir o novo PPA importado.= </p> <pre class=3D"wp-block-code language-bash" tabindex=3D"0"><code lang=3D"bas= h" class=3D"language-bash"><span class=3D"token function">sudo</span> <span= class=3D"token function">apt</span> update</code></pre> <p>Agora voc=C3=AA pode instalar o Python 3.7 executando o seguinte c=C3=B3= digo:</p> <pre class=3D"wp-block-code language-bash" tabindex=3D"0"><code lang=3D"bas= h" class=3D"language-bash"><span class=3D"token function">sudo</span> <span= class=3D"token function">apt</span> <span class=3D"token function">install= </span> python3.7 -y</code></pre> <p>Para verificar a instala=C3=A7=C3=A3o e a vers=C3=A3o de compila=C3=A7= =C3=A3o do Python 3.7, fa=C3=A7a o seguinte.</p> <pre class=3D"wp-block-code language-bash" tabindex=3D"0"><code lang=3D"bas= h" class=3D"language-bash">python3.7 --version</code></pre> <p class=3D"gt-block"><em>Exemplo de sa=C3=ADda:</em></p> <div class=3D"wp-block-image"><figure class=3D"aligncenter size-full"><img = width=3D"759" height=3D"191" src=3D"https://www.linuxcapable.com/wp-content= /uploads/2022/03/python-version-output-3.7-ubuntu-20.04-lts.png" alt=3D"Com= o instalar o Python 3.7 no Ubuntu 20.04 LTS" class=3D"wp-image-24736"></fig= ure></div> <div class=3D"code-block code-block-9 code-block-block-9" style=3D"margin: = 0px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both; min-height: 310p=
